<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Kroger is a retailer in the United States, operating supermarkets and multi-department stores under two dozen local banner names.&#160; Acquisition Sub is a direct wholly owned subsidiary of Kroger, and was recently incorporated for the purpose of acquiring all of the issued and outstanding shares of the common stock, par value $0.00001 per share, of Vitacost (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Shares</u></font>&#8221;) and consummating the transactions contemplated by the Merger Agreement (defined below in Item 4) and, to date, has engaged and is expected to engage in no other activities other than those incidental to the Offer (defined below in Item 4), the Merger (defined below in Item 4) and the Merger Agreement.&#160; Until immediately prior to the time Acquisition Sub purchases Shares pursuant to the Offer, it is not anticipated that Acquisition Sub will have any significant assets or liabilities.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The name, business address, present principal occupation or employment and citizenship of each executive officer and director and each controlling person of Kroger and Acquisition Sub, and each executive officer and director of any corporation or other person ultimately in control of Kroger and Acquisition Sub, are set forth on <font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Annex A</u></font> attached hereto.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">During the last five years, none of Kroger or Acquisition Sub, and to the best knowledge of each of Kroger and Acquisition Sub, none of the persons on <font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Annex A</u></font>, (a) has been convicted in a criminal proceeding (excluding traffic violations or similar misdemeanors) or (b) has been a party to a civil proceeding of a judicial or administrative body of competent jurisdiction and as a result of such proceeding was or is subject to a judgment, decree or final order enjoining future violations of, or prohibiting or mandating activities subject to, federal or state securities laws or finding any violation with respect to such laws.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The Reporting Persons have entered into a Joint Filing Agreement, dated July 10<!--Anchor-->, 2014, a copy of which is attached as Exhibit 1 hereto, pursuant to which the Reporting Persons have agreed to file this statement jointly in accordance with the provisions of Rule 13d&#8722;1(k)(1) of the Exchange Act.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<td style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; WIDTH: auto; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Source and Amount of Funds or Other Consideration.</td>

</table>
</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Pursuant to, and subject to the terms and conditions contained in, the Tender and Support Agreements described in Item 4 of this statement, the Reporting Persons may be deemed to have acquired beneficial ownership of the Subject Shares (as defined below) by virtue of the execution of the Tender and Support Agreements (as defined in Item 4 below) by Kroger, Acquisition Sub and certain stockholders of Vitacost. As a result of Acquisition Sub being its direct wholly owned subsidiary, Kroger may be deemed to share beneficial ownership of the Subject Shares that Acquisition Sub may be deemed to beneficially own. No payments were made by or on behalf of the Reporting Persons in connection with the execution of the Merger Agreement (as defined in Item 4 below) or the execution of the Tender and Support Agreements. It is currently anticipated that Kroger or Acquisition Sub will finance the acquisition of Shares in the Offer (as defined below in Item 4) with Kroger&#8217;s cash on hand, and/or debt.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left">
<table style="WIDTH: 100%; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt" class="DSPFListTable" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0">
<tr>
<td style="WIDTH: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold; align: right">Item 4.</td>
<td style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; WIDTH: auto; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Purpose of Transaction.</td>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Merger Agreement and Tender Offer</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, Serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt" id="DSPFPageNumberArea">4</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #fb2222; MARGIN: 4px 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; COLOR: #fb2222; CLEAR: both; BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px" id="DSPFPageBreak" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">On July 1, 2014, Kroger and Acquisition Sub entered into an Agreement and Plan of Merger (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Merger Agreement</u></font>&#8221;) with Vitacost.&#160; Under the Merger Agreement, among other things, Acquisition Sub will commence a tender offer (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Offer</u></font>&#8221;) to purchase all of the Shares, at a price per Share of $8.00 in cash, without interest (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Offer Price</u></font>&#8221;). Upon successful completion of the Offer, and subject to the terms and conditions of the Merger Agreement, Acquisition Sub will be merged with and into Vitacost (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Merger</u></font>&#8221;), and Vitacost will survive the Merger as a direct wholly owned subsidiary of Kroger (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Surviving Corporation</u></font>&#8221;).&#160; It is anticipated that, the Merger will be governed by Section 251(h) of the General Corporation Law of the State of Delaware (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>DGCL</u></font>&#8221;), with no stockholder vote required to consummate the Merger.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">At the effective time of the Merger (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Effective Time</u></font>&#8221;), each Share issued and outstanding immediately prior to the Effective Time (other than Shares owned by Vitacost, Kroger or Acquisition Sub or their respective wholly owned subsidiaries, or by stockholders who have validly exercised their appraisal rights under Delaware law) will be converted automatically into the right to receive the Offer Price (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Merger Consideration</u></font>&#8221;). Options to purchase Shares that are outstanding, whether or not vested, immediately prior to the Effective Time, will be canceled and, provided that the per share exercise price of such options exceeds the Offer Price, converted automatically into the right to receive, in exchange for the cancellation of such options, an amount of cash, without interest, equal to the product obtained by multiplying (x) the aggregate number of Shares that were issuable upon exercise of such option immediately prior to the Effective Time and (y) the Offer Price, less the per share exercise price of such option.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Under the Merger Agreement, and upon the terms and conditions contained therein, Acquisition Sub is obligated to commence the Offer as promptly as reasonably practicable after July 1, 2014, the date of the Merger Agreement. The Offer will remain open for at least 20 business days, which period may be extended under certain circumstances described in the Merger Agreement. Acquisition Sub&#8217;s obligation to accept for payment and pay for any Shares tendered in the Offer is subject to certain conditions, including (i) there having been validly tendered and not validly withdrawn prior to the expiration of the Offer a number of Shares that represents at least a majority of the total number of Shares outstanding on a fully diluted basis, (ii) the waiting period (and any extension thereof) applicable to the Offer under the Hart&#8722;Scott&#8722;Rodino Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended, and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder having been expired or terminated prior to the Expiration Date, (iii) the absence of any material adverse effect with respect to Vitacost and (iv) certain other customary conditions. The Offer is not subject to a financing condition.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In the event the Merger cannot be effected pursuant to Section 251(h) of the DGCL, Vitacost granted to Acquisition Sub under the Merger Agreement an irrevocable option (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Top&#8722;Up Option</u></font>&#8221;), exercisable after the consummation of the Offer and prior to the Effective Time, to purchase at a price per Share equal to the Offer Price up to that number of newly issued Shares (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Top&#8722;Up Shares</u></font>&#8221;) from Vitacost at a per Share purchase price equal to the Offer Price that, when added to the number of Shares owned by Kroger and Acquisition Sub at the time of exercise of the Top&#8722;Up Option, constitutes one hundred shares more than 90% of the Shares outstanding immediately after the issuance of the Top&#8722;Up Shares on a fully diluted basis.&#160; If Kroger and Acquisition Sub shall acquire, together with the Shares held by Kroger, Acquisition Sub and any other subsidiary of Kroger, at least 90% of the outstanding Shares, they will complete the Merger through the &#8220;short form&#8221; procedures available under Section 253 of the DGCL.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The Merger Agreement also provides that, upon payment for Shares representing at least a majority of the total number of outstanding shares of Vitacost&#8217;s common stock on a fully diluted basis, Acquisition Sub will be entitled to designate a number of directors to the board of directors of Vitacost (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Vitacost Board</u></font>&#8221;) in proportion with the percentage of the Shares it owns following the Offer. Between such time and the Effective Time, the Vitacost Board will have at least two directors who are directors of Vitacost on the date of the Merger Agreement and who are independent directors for purposes of the continued listing requirements of The Nasdaq Global Market.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Kroger, Acquisition Sub and Vitacost have made customary representations and warranties in the Merger Agreement and agreed to certain customary covenants, including covenants regarding operation of the business of Vitacost and its subsidiaries prior to the closing. In addition, Vitacost has made certain covenants restricting Vitacost from soliciting, or providing information or entering into discussions concerning, proposals relating to alternative business combination transactions. However, Vitacost may take certain specified actions in response to an unsolicited proposal that the Vitacost Board reasonably determines in good faith is, or could reasonably be expected to lead to, a proposal superior to the transactions contemplated in the Merger Agreement, if failure to take such actions would be reasonably expected to result in a breach of the Vitacost Board&#8217;s fiduciary duties and other specified conditions are met. In such circumstances, and subject to certain obligations to notify Kroger and to other rights granted to Kroger, including the right to require Vitacost to engage in good faith negotiations for an amendment to the Merger Agreement, the Vitacost Board may cause Vitacost to terminate the Merger Agreement in response to such superior proposal. Upon termination of the Merger Agreement in such circumstances or other specified circumstances, Vitacost will be required to pay Kroger a termination fee of $9,275,000.&#160; If Kroger terminates the Merger Agreement as a result of a breach of Vitacost&#8217;s representations or warranties or Vitacost&#8217;s failure to perform in any material respect under the Merger Agreement, which causes a failure of the Offer conditions and which is not cured, then Vitacost is required to pay Kroger&#8217;s out of pocket fees and expenses.</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, Serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt" id="DSPFPageNumberArea">5</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #fb2222; MARGIN: 4px 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; COLOR: #fb2222; CLEAR: both; BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px" id="DSPFPageBreak" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div style="TEXT-INDENT: 36pt">The Merger Agreement has been provided solely to inform investors of its terms. The representations, warranties and covenants contained in the Merger Agreement were made only for the purposes of such agreement and as of specific dates, were made solely for the benefit of the parties to the Merger Agreement and may be intended not as statements of fact, but rather as a way of allocating risk to one of the parties if those statements prove to be inaccurate. In addition, such representations, warranties and covenants may have been qualified by certain disclosures not reflected in the text of the Merger Agreement and may apply standards of materiality in a way that is different from what may be viewed as material by stockholders of, or other investors in, Vitacost. Vitacost&#8217;s stockholders and other investors are not third&#8722;party beneficiaries under the Merger Agreement and should not rely on the representations, warranties and covenants or any descriptions thereof as characterizations of the actual state of facts or conditions of Vitacost, Kroger, Acquisition Sub or any of their respective subsidiaries or affiliates.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; FONT-STYLE: italic; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Tender and Support Agreements</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">In connection with the execution and delivery of the Merger Agreement, Kroger and Acquisition Sub entered into tender and support agreements, dated as of July 1, 2014 (the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Tender and Support Agreements</u></font>&#8221;), with each of Jeffrey Horowitz, JHH Capital, LLC, Great Hill Investors, LLC, Great Hill Equity Partners III, L.P. and Great Hill Equity Partners IV, L.P. (collectively, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Supporting Stockholders</u></font>&#8221;). Pursuant to the Tender and Support Agreements, the Supporting Stockholders agreed, subject to certain limited specified exceptions, to tender, and not withdraw, all outstanding Shares beneficially owned by them, or acquired by them after such date (collectively, the &#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Subject Shares</u></font>&#8221;).&#160; In addition, such stockholders have agreed, subject to certain exceptions, to refrain from disposing of the Subject Shares and soliciting alternative acquisition proposals to the Merger. The Tender and Support Agreements will terminate upon certain circumstances, including upon termination of the Merger Agreement.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Based upon information provided by the Supporting Stockholders, as of July 1, 2014, the Subject Shares included: (i) 2,022,500 Shares beneficially owned by Jeffrey Horowitz, (ii) 3,049,013 Shares beneficially owned by JHH Capital, LLC; (iii) 19,489 Shares beneficially owned by Great Hill Investors, LLC; (iv) 4,398,828 Shares beneficially owned by Great Hill Equity Partners III, L.P.; and (v) 2,306,497 Shares beneficially owned by Great Hill Equity Partners IV, L.P. The Reporting Persons may be deemed to have acquired shared voting and disposition power with respect to the Subject Shares by reason of the execution and delivery of the Tender and Support Agreements by Kroger and Acquisition Sub. As a result of Acquisition Sub being its direct wholly owned subsidiary, Kroger may be deemed to share beneficial ownership of the Subject Shares that Acquisition Sub may be deemed to beneficially own.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The foregoing descriptions of the Merger Agreement and Tender and Support Agreements do not purport to be complete and are qualified in their entirety by reference to such agreements. The Merger Agreement and Tender Support Agreements are referenced herein as Exhibits 2 through 7 and are incorporated by reference into this Item 4.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">The purpose of the transactions described above is for Kroger, through Acquisition Sub, to acquire control of, and the entire equity interest in, Vitacost. Kroger required that the Supporting Stockholders agree to enter into the Tender and Support Agreements to induce Kroger and Acquisition Sub to enter into the Merger Agreement and to consummate the transactions contemplated by the Merger Agreement, including the Offer and the Merger. Upon consummation of the Merger, Vitacost will become a wholly owned subsidiary of Kroger, the Shares will cease to be freely traded or listed, Vitacost common stock will be de&#8722;registered under the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, and Kroger will control the board of directors of Vitacost and will make such other changes in the charter, bylaws, capitalization, management and business of Vitacost as set forth in the Merger Agreement and/or as may be appropriate in its judgment (subject to certain limitations).</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, Serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt" id="DSPFPageNumberArea">6</div>

</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Except as set forth or incorporated by reference in this Schedule 13D, Kroger and Acquisition Sub have no plans or proposals that relate to or would result in any of the transactions described in subparagraphs (a) through (j) of Item 4 of Schedule 13D.</div>

<td style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; WIDTH: auto; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; VERTICAL-ALIGN: top">As a result of the Tender and Support Agreements, as of July 1, 2014, the Reporting Persons may be deemed, for purposes of Rule 13d&#8722;3 under the Exchange Act (&#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Rule 13d&#8722;3</u></font>&#8221;), to share with the Supporting Stockholders the power to vote or direct the voting or disposition of the 11,796,327 Subject Shares, and thus, for the purpose of Rule 13d&#8722;3, the Reporting Persons may be deemed to be the beneficial owners of an aggregate of 11,796,327 Shares, which constitutes approximately 32.0% of the Shares (as represented by Vitacost in the Merger Agreement). Including only options to purchase Shares exercisable on July 1, 2014 or becoming exercisable within 60 days thereafter, the Supporting Stockholders beneficially owned, in the aggregate, 11,258,327 Shares (representing approximately 30.9 percent of all outstanding Shares after giving effect to the exercise of such options) as of July 1, 2014.&#160; Except as set forth in this Item 5(a), none of the Reporting Persons, and, to the best knowledge of the Reporting Persons, none of the persons named in <font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><u>Annex A</u></font> hereto beneficially owns any Shares. The Reporting Persons hereby disclaim that they constitute a &#8220;group&#8221; (within the meaning of Section 13(d)(3) of the Exchange Act) with the Supporting Stockholders and hereby disclaim beneficial ownership of any Shares beneficially owned by the Supporting Stockholders or any of their affiliates including, without limitation, the Subject Shares. Neither the filing of this Schedule 13D nor any of its contents shall be deemed to constitute an admission by the Reporting Persons that it is the beneficial owner of any Shares, and the Reporting Persons expressly disclaim all beneficial ownership of such Shares.</td>

<div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Exhibit 3</div>

<div>&#160;</div>

<div>
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TENDER AND SUPPORT AGREEMENT</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->TENDER AND SUPPORT AGREEMENT, dated as of July 1, 2014 (this &#8220;<!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Agreement</font>&#8221;), among The Kroger Co., an <!--Anchor-->Ohio corporation (&#8220;<!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent</font>&#8221;), Vigor Acquisition Corp., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Acquisition Sub</font>&#8221;), and the Person listed as &#8220;<!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8221; on the signature page hereto (&#8220;<!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Stockholder</font>&#8221;).</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor-->WHEREAS, as a condition and inducement to <!--Anchor-->Parent&#8217;s and Acquisition Sub&#8217;s willingness to enter into an <!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated as of the date <!--Anchor-->hereof (the &#8220;<!--Anchor--><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), with Vitacost.com, Inc. a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221;), <!--Anchor-->Parent has requested <!--Anchor-->Stockholder, and <!--Anchor-->Stockholder has agreed, to enter into this <!--Anchor-->Agreement with respect to all shares of common stock, par value $0.00001 per share, of the <!--Anchor-->Company that Stockholder Beneficially Owns (as defined in Section 6.10 below) at any time during the <!--Anchor-->Support Period (as defined in Section 6.10 below).</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">NOW, THEREFORE, the parties hereto agree as follows:</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->ARTICLE 1</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor-->Agreement to Tender</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.01</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Tender of Shares</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder agrees: <!--Anchor-->(i) to promptly (and, in any event, not later than five (5) Business Days after commencement of the Offer) validly tender or cause to be validly tendered into the Offer, pursuant to and in accordance with the terms of the Offer and Rule 14d-2 under the <!--Anchor-->Exchange Act, all of the outstanding Company Shares<!--Anchor--> Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder (free and clear of any Liens or restrictions, except for any applicable restrictions on transfer under the Securities Act and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder that would not in any event prevent Stockholder from tendering Stockholder&#8217;s Company Shares in accordance with this Agreement or otherwise complying with Stockholder&#8217;s obligations under this Agreement); and <!--Anchor-->(ii) if <!--Anchor-->Stockholder acquires Beneficial Ownership of any additional outstanding Company Shares<!--Anchor--> during the Support Period, to promptly (and, in any event, not later than three (3) Business Days after <!--Anchor-->Stockholder acquires <!--Anchor-->Beneficial Ownership of such additional outstanding Company Shares) validly tender or cause to be validly tendered into the Offer, pursuant to and in accordance with the terms of the Offer, all of such additional Company Shares (free and clear of any Liens or restrictions, except for any applicable restrictions on transfer under the Securities Act and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder that would not in any event prevent Stockholder from tendering Stockholder&#8217;s Company Shares in accordance with this Agreement or otherwise complying with Stockholder&#8217;s obligations under this Agreement).&#160; Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement to the contrary, (a) the Stockholder shall not have any obligation under this Section 1.01 to tender into the Offer if the tender would give rise to liability (including disgorgement) under Section 16(b) of the Exchange Act, and (b) nothing herein shall require Stockholder to exercise any Company Option or other equity award or require Stockholder to purchase any Company Shares pursuant to any Company Warrant or otherwise, and nothing herein shall prohibit Stockholder from exercising any Company Option or Company Warrants held by such Stockholder as of the date of this Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="text-align: justify; text-indent: 36pt; font-family: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt;"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.02</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">No Withdrawal</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder agrees not to withdraw, and not to cause or permit to be withdrawn, any Company Shares<!--Anchor--> from the Offer unless and until (i) the Offer expires without <!--Anchor-->Acquisition Sub having accepted for payment any Company Shares tendered in the Offer or (ii) termination of this Agreement in accordance with Section 6.03 hereof.</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #fb2222; MARGIN: 4px 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; COLOR: #fb2222; CLEAR: both; BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px" id="DSPFPageBreak" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.03</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Conditional Obligation</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder acknowledges and agrees that Acquisition Sub&#8217;s obligation to accept for payment <!--Anchor-->Company Shares tendered into the Offer, <!--Anchor-->including any Company Shares tendered by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder, is subject to the terms and conditions of the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement and the <!--Anchor-->Offer.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><!--Anchor-->ARTICLE 2</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor-->Voting Agreement; Grant of Proxy</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 2.01</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Voting </font><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Agreement</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder hereby agrees that, during the <!--Anchor-->Support Period, <!--Anchor-->Stockholder will not vote any outstanding Company Shares <!--Anchor-->Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder in favor of, or consent to, and will vote against and not consent to, the approval of any <!--Anchor-->(i) Acquisition Proposal, <!--Anchor-->(ii) reorganization, recapitalization, dissolution, liquidation or winding-up of the <!--Anchor-->Company or any other extraordinary transaction involving the <!--Anchor-->Company other than the Merger, <!--Anchor-->(iii) corporate action the consummation of which would frustrate the purposes, or prevent or materially delay the consummation, of any <!--Anchor-->of the transactions contemplated by the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement or <!--Anchor-->(iv) other matter relating to, or in connection with, any of the foregoing matters. Stockholder shall use its commercially reasonable efforts to ensure that, during the Support Period, any other Person having voting power with respect to any outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by Stockholder will not vote any such shares in favor of or consent to, and will vote against, the approval of the matters described in clauses (i) through (iv) of the preceding sentence.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 2.02</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Irrevocable Proxy</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder hereby revokes (or agrees to cause to be revoked) any and all previous proxies granted with respect to the outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder.&#160; By entering into this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, <!--Anchor-->Stockholder hereby grants a proxy appointing <!--Anchor-->Parent as <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s attorney-in-fact and proxy, with full power of substitution, for and in <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s name, to vote, express consent or dissent, or otherwise to utilize such voting power in the manner contemplated by Section 2.01<!--Anchor--> above as <!--Anchor-->Parent or its proxy or substitute shall, in <!--Anchor-->Parent&#8217;s sole discretion, deem proper with respect to the outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder.&#160; The proxy granted by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder pursuant to this Article 2<!--Anchor--> is irrevocable and is granted in consideration of <!--Anchor-->Parent and Acquisition Sub entering into this <!--Anchor-->Agreement and the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement and incurring certain related fees and expenses.&#160; The proxy granted by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder shall not be exercised to vote, consent or act on any matter except as contemplated by Section 2.01<!--Anchor--> above.&#160; The proxy granted by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder shall be revoked, terminated and of no further force or effect, automatically and without further action, upon termination of this <!--Anchor-->Agreement in accordance with Section 6.03 hereof.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Covenants of <!--Anchor-->Stockholder</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor-->Stockholder hereby covenants and agrees that:</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 5.01</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; No Proxies for, Encumbrances on or Disposition of Shares</font>.&#160; During the <!--Anchor-->Support Period, except pursuant to the terms of this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, <!--Anchor-->Stockholder shall not, without the prior <!--Anchor-->written consent of <!--Anchor-->Parent, directly or indirectly, (a) grant any proxies, or enter into any voting trust or other Contract, with respect to the voting of any Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder, (b) sell, assign, transfer, tender, encumber or otherwise dispose of, or enter into any Contract with respect to the direct or indirect sale, assignment, transfer, tender, encumbrance or other disposition of, any such Company Shares or (c) take any other action that would make any representation or warranty of <!--Anchor-->Stockholder contained <!--Anchor-->herein untrue or incorrect in any material respect or in any way restrict, limit or interfere in any material respect with the performance of <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s obligations <!--Anchor-->hereunder <!--Anchor-->or <!--Anchor-->the transactions contemplated hereby or by the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement, or seek to do or solicit any of the foregoing actions, or cause or permit any other Person to take any of the foregoing actions, and agrees to notify <!--Anchor-->Parent and <!--Anchor-->Acquisition Sub promptly, and to provide all material details reasonably requested by <!--Anchor-->Parent or Acquisition Sub, if <!--Anchor-->Stockholder shall be approached or solicited, directly or indirectly, by any Person with respect to any of the foregoing.&#160; Without limiting the generality of the foregoing, during the Support Period, Stockholder shall not tender, agree to tender or cause or permit to be tendered any Company Shares Beneficially Owned by Stockholder into or otherwise in connection with any tender or exchange offer, except pursuant to the Offer.&#160; Notwithstanding the foregoing, Stockholder may transfer Company Shares held by Stockholder to a trust for the benefit of Stockholder; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">provided</font> that a transfer referred to in this sentence shall be permitted only if, as a precondition to such transfer, the transferee agrees in a writing, reasonably satisfactory in form and substance to Parent, to be bound by all of the terms of this Agreement.</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, Serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt" id="DSPFPageNumberArea">4</div>

</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 5.02</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Other Offers</font>.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder (in Stockholder&#8217;s capacity as such), will not authorize or permit any of his Representatives to, and Stockholder shall instruct each such Representative not to, directly or indirectly, take any of the following actions: <!--Anchor-->(i) solicit, initiate, cause or induce the making, submission or announcement of, or knowingly encourage, facilitate or assist, an Acquisition Proposal;<!--Anchor--> (ii) furnish to any Person (other than Parent, Acquisition Sub or any designees of Parent or Acquisition Sub) any non-public information relating to the Company or any of its Subsidiaries, or afford to any Person (other than Parent, Acquisition Sub or any designees of Parent or Acquisition Sub) access to the business, properties, assets, books, records or other non-public information, or to any personnel, of the Company or any of its Subsidiaries, in any such case with the intent to induce the making, submission or announcement of, or the intent to encourage, facilitate or assist, an Acquisition Proposal or any inquiries or the making of any proposal that would reasonably be expected to lead to an Acquisition Proposal; (iii) participate or engage in discussions or negotiations with any Person with respect to an Acquisition Proposal; or (iv) enter into any Contract contemplating or otherwise relating to an Acquisition Transaction.<!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->&#160; Stockholder (in Stockholder&#8217;s capacity as such) shall, and shall cause his Representatives to immediately cease any and all existing discussions or negotiations with any Persons conducted heretofore with respect to any Acquisition Proposal, and shall request the return from all such Persons or the destruction by such Persons of all copies of confidential information previously provided to such Persons by Stockholder or his Representatives.&#160; Stockholder shall promptly notify Parent if he becomes aware of any receipt by Stockholder or his Representatives of (i) any Acquisition Proposal, (ii) any request for information that would reasonably be expected to lead to an Acquisition Proposal, or (iii) any inquiry with respect to, or which would reasonably be expected to lead to, any Acquisition Proposal, the terms and conditions of such Acquisition Proposal, request or inquiry, and the identity of the Person or group making any such Acquisition Proposal, request or inquiry (and shall include with such notice copies of any written materials received from or on behalf of such Person relating to such Acquisition Proposal).&#160; Stockholder shall keep Parent reasonably informed of the status and material terms of any such Acquisition Proposal known to Stockholder, request or inquiry (and Stockholder shall provide Parent with copies of any additional written materials received by it that relate to such Acquisition Proposal, inquiry or request).&#160; Notwithstanding the foregoing, nothing herein shall limit or affect any actions taken by Stockholder (or any affiliated officer or director of the Company) in compliance with the Merger Agreement, including taking any of the foregoing actions that would be permitted to be taken by the Company pursuant to the Merger Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 5.03</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder shall not, and shall cause his Representatives, if any, not to, directly or indirectly, make any press release, public announcement or other public communication that criticizes or disparages this <!--Anchor-->Agreement or the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement or any <!--Anchor-->of <!--Anchor-->the transactions contemplated hereby and thereby, without the prior <!--Anchor-->written consent of <!--Anchor-->Parent.&#160; <!--Anchor-->Stockholder hereby <!--Anchor-->(i) consents to and authorizes the publication and disclosure by <!--Anchor-->Parent, <!--Anchor-->Acquisition Sub and the <!--Anchor-->Company (<!--Anchor-->including in the <!--Anchor-->Schedule TO, the <!--Anchor-->Schedule 14D-9 or any other publicly filed documents relating to the <!--Anchor-->Merger, the Offer or any other transaction contemplated by the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement) of: (a) <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s identity; (b) <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s <!--Anchor-->Beneficial Ownership <!--Anchor-->of <!--Anchor-->Company Shares; and (c) the nature of <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s commitments, arrangements and understandings under this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, and any other information that <!--Anchor-->Parent, <!--Anchor-->Acquisition Sub or the <!--Anchor-->Company determines to be necessary in any SEC disclosure document in connection with the Offer, the <!--Anchor-->Merger or any of the other transactions contemplated by the <!--Anchor-->Merger Agreement and <!--Anchor-->(ii) agrees as promptly as practicable to notify <!--Anchor-->Parent, <!--Anchor-->Acquisition Sub and the <!--Anchor-->Company of any required corrections with respect to any <!--Anchor-->written information supplied by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder specifically for use in any such disclosure document.&#160; Notwithstanding the foregoing, nothing herein shall limit or affect any actions taken by Stockholder (or any affiliated officer or director of the Company) in compliance with the Merger Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><!--Anchor-->ARTICLE 6</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Miscellaneous</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.01</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Other Definitional and Interpretative Provisions.</font>&#160; Unless specified otherwise, in this <!--Anchor-->Agreement the obligations of any party hereto consisting of more than one <!--Anchor-->Person are joint and several.&#160; The words &#8220;<!--Anchor-->hereof,&#8221; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Submission to Jurisdiction</font>.&#160; Each party to this <!--Anchor-->Agreement hereby irrevocably and unconditionally <!--Anchor-->(i) consents to the submission to the exclusive jurisdiction of the <!--Anchor-->Court of Chancery of the State of <!--Anchor-->Delaware sitting in <!--Anchor-->Wilmington, <!--Anchor-->Delaware for any <!--Anchor-->Legal Proceedings arising out of or relating to this <!--Anchor-->Agreement <!--Anchor-->or <!--Anchor-->the transactions contemplated hereby, <!--Anchor-->(ii) agrees not to commence any Legal Proceeding relating thereto except in such court and in accordance with the provisions of this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, <!--Anchor-->(iii) agrees that service of any process, summons, notice or document by <!--Anchor--><!--Anchor-->U.S. registered mail, or otherwise in the manner provided for notices in Section 6.12 <!--Anchor-->hereof, shall be effective service of process for any such Legal Proceeding brought against it in any such court, <!--Anchor-->(iv) waives, to the fullest extent it may legally and effectively do so, any objection which it may now or hereafter have to the laying of venue of any such Legal Proceeding in such courts and <!--Anchor-->(v) agrees not to plead or claim in any court that any such Legal Proceeding brought in any such court has been brought in an inconvenient forum.&#160; <div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.14</font><font style="FONT-SIZE: 5.14pt">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;</font><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Waiver</font>&#160;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">of</font>&#160;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Jury</font>&#160;<font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Trial</font>.&#160; EACH OF THE PARTIES HERETO HEREBY IRREVOCABLY WAIVES ANY AND ALL RIGHT TO TRIAL BY JURY IN ANY PROCEEDING ARISING OUT OF OR RELATED TO THIS <!--Anchor-->AGREEMENT OR ANY <!--Anchor-->OF <!--Anchor-->THE TRANSACTIONS CONTEMPLATED HEREBY.</font></div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.15</font>.&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Rules of Construction</font>.&#160; The parties hereto agree that they have been represented by counsel during the negotiation and execution of this <!--Anchor-->Agreement and, therefore, waive the application of any law, regulation, holding or rule of construction providing that ambiguities in an <!--Anchor-->agreement or other document will be construed against the party drafting such <!--Anchor-->agreement or document.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.16</font>.&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Waiver</font>.&#160; No failure on the part of any party to exercise <!--Anchor-->any <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy under this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, and no delay on the part of any party in exercising <!--Anchor-->any <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy under this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, shall operate as a waiver of such <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy; and no single or partial exercise of any such <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy shall preclude any other or further exercise thereof or of any other <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy.&#160; A party hereto shall not be deemed to have waived any claim arising out of this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, or <!--Anchor-->any <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy under this <!--Anchor-->Agreement, unless the waiver of such claim, <!--Anchor-->power, right, privilege or remedy is expressly set forth in a <!--Anchor-->written instrument duly executed and delivered on behalf of such party; and any such waiver shall not be applicable or have any effect except in the specific instance in which it is given.</div>

<div><br>
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.17</font>.&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">No Ownership Interest.</font>&#160; All rights, ownership and economic benefits of and relating to <!--Anchor-->the <!--Anchor-->Company Shares <!--Anchor-->Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder at a given time shall remain vested in and belong to <!--Anchor-->Stockholder as of such time, and <!--Anchor-->Parent shall have no authority to exercise any power or authority to direct <!--Anchor-->Stockholder in the voting of any of the Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <!--Anchor-->Stockholder, except as otherwise specifically provided <!--Anchor-->herein, or in the performance of <!--Anchor-->Stockholder&#8217;s duties or responsibilities as a <!--Anchor-->stockholder of the <!--Anchor-->Company.</div>

<div style="MARGIN-TOP: 10pt; MARGIN-BOTTOM: 10pt; CLEAR: both" id="DSPFPageBreakArea">
<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: 'Times New Roman', Times, Serif; FONT-SIZE: 8pt" id="DSPFPageNumberArea">10</div>

<hr style="PAGE-BREAK-AFTER: always; BORDER-RIGHT-WIDTH: 0px; BACKGROUND-COLOR: #fb2222; MARGIN: 4px 0px; WIDTH: 100%; BORDER-TOP-WIDTH: 0px; BORDER-BOTTOM-WIDTH: 0px; HEIGHT: 2px; COLOR: #fb2222; CLEAR: both; BORDER-LEFT-WIDTH: 0px" id="DSPFPageBreak" noshade="noshade">
</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 6.18</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Entire </font><!--Anchor--><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Agreement</font>.&#160; This <!--Anchor-->Agreement constitutes the entire <!--Anchor-->agreement among the parties hereto with respect to the subject matter <!--Anchor-->hereof and supersedes all other prior agreements and understandings, both <!--Anchor-->written and oral, among the parties hereto with respect to the subject matter <!--Anchor-->hereof.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Exhibit 4</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: right; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">EXECUTION COPY</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">TENDER AND SUPPORT AGREEMENT</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="ElohO"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="EloyO"><!--Anchor--></a>TENDER AND SUPPORT AGREEMENT, dated as of July 1, 2014 (this &#8220;<a name="El35O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Agreement</font>&#8221;), among The Kroger Co., an <a name="El2eO"><!--Anchor--></a>Ohio corporation (&#8220;<a name="El37O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Parent</font>&#8221;), Vigor Acquisition Corp., a Delaware corporation (&#8220;<font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Acquisition Sub</font>&#8221;), and the Person listed as &#8220;<a name="El2dO"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="ElqkO"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder&#8221; on the signature page hereto (&#8220;<a name="El3bO"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Stockholder</font>&#8221;).</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Elom1O"><!--Anchor--></a>WHEREAS, as a condition and inducement to <a name="El2c1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent&#8217;s and Acquisition Sub&#8217;s willingness to enter into an <a name="El231O"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="Elni1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated as of the date <a name="El2e1O"><!--Anchor--></a>hereof (the &#8220;<a name="El3zO"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="Elnj1O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Merger Agreement</font>&#8221;), with Vitacost.com, Inc. a Delaware corporation (the &#8220;<a name="El3fO"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold">Company</font>&#8221;), <a name="El2a1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent has requested <a name="El241O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder, and <a name="El2d1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder has agreed, to enter into this <a name="El251O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement with respect to all shares of common stock, par value $0.00001 per share, of the <a name="El2b1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Company that Stockholder Beneficially Owns (as defined in Section 6.10 below) at any time during the <a name="El261O"><!--Anchor--></a>Support Period (as defined in Section 6.10 below).</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">NOW, THEREFORE, the parties hereto agree as follows:</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><a name="Eloo1O"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="Elop1O"><!--Anchor--></a>ARTICLE 1</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="El2r1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement to Tender</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Elot1O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.01</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Tender of Shares</font>.&#160; <a name="El2w1O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder agrees: <a name="Eloz1O"><!--Anchor--></a>(i) to promptly (and, in any event, not later than five (5) Business Days after commencement of the Offer) validly tender or cause to be validly tendered into the Offer, pursuant to and in accordance with the terms of the Offer and Rule 14d-2 under the <a name="Elr52O"><!--Anchor--></a>Exchange Act, all of the outstanding Company Shares<a name="El212O"><!--Anchor--></a> Beneficially Owned by <a name="El222O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder (free and clear of any Liens or restrictions, except for any applicable restrictions on transfer under the Securities Act and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder that would not in any event prevent Stockholder from tendering Stockholder&#8217;s Company Shares in accordance with this Agreement or otherwise complying with Stockholder&#8217;s obligations under this Agreement); and <a name="Elo62O"><!--Anchor--></a>(ii) if <a name="El272O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder acquires Beneficial Ownership of any additional outstanding Company Shares<a name="El292O"><!--Anchor--></a> during the Support Period, to promptly (and, in any event, not later than three (3) Business Days after <a name="El2b2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder acquires <a name="El2c2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Beneficial Ownership of such additional outstanding Company Shares) validly tender or cause to be validly tendered into the Offer, pursuant to and in accordance with the terms of the Offer, all of such additional Company Shares (free and clear of any Liens or restrictions, except for any applicable restrictions on transfer under the Securities Act and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder that would not in any event prevent Stockholder from tendering Stockholder&#8217;s Company Shares in accordance with this Agreement or otherwise complying with Stockholder&#8217;s obligations under this Agreement).&#160; Notwithstanding anything in this Agreement to the contrary, (a) the Stockholder shall not have any obligation under this Section 1.01 to tender into the Offer if the tender would give rise to liability (including disgorgement) under Section 16(b) of the Exchange Act, and (b) nothing herein shall require Stockholder to exercise any Company Option or other equity award or require Stockholder to purchase any Company Shares pursuant to any Company Warrant or otherwise, and nothing herein shall prohibit Stockholder from exercising any Company Option or Company Warrants held by such Stockholder as of the date of this Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Eloh2O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.02</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">No Withdrawal</font>.&#160; <a name="El2j2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder agrees not to withdraw, and not to cause or permit to be withdrawn, any Company Shares<a name="El2n2O"><!--Anchor--></a> from the Offer unless and until (i) the Offer expires without <a name="El2k2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Acquisition Sub having accepted for payment any Company Shares tendered in the Offer or (ii) termination of this Agreement in accordance with Section 6.03 hereof.<!--Anchor--></div>

</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 1.03</font>&#160; <font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Conditional Obligation</font>.&#160; <a name="El2u2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder acknowledges and agrees that Acquisition Sub&#8217;s obligation to accept for payment <a name="El2_2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Company Shares tendered into the Offer, <a name="El213O"><!--Anchor--></a>including any Company Shares tendered by <a name="El2x2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder, is subject to the terms and conditions of the <a name="El2y2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Merger Agreement and the <a name="El2z2O"><!--Anchor--></a>Offer.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><a name="Elo73O"><!--Anchor--></a>ARTICLE 2</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="_Ref4903874"><!--Anchor--></a>Voting Agreement; Grant of Proxy</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-VARIANT: small-caps; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Eloa3O"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="_Ref4903854"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 2.01</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Voting </font><a name="El2c3O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Agreement</font>.&#160; <a name="El2d3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder hereby agrees that, during the <a name="El2e3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Support Period, <a name="El2h3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder will not vote any outstanding Company Shares <a name="El2f3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Beneficially Owned by <a name="El2g3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder in favor of, or consent to, and will vote against and not consent to, the approval of any <a name="Elom3O"><!--Anchor--></a>(i) Acquisition Proposal, <a name="Elon3O"><!--Anchor--></a>(ii) reorganization, recapitalization, dissolution, liquidation or winding-up of the <a name="El2o3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Company or any other extraordinary transaction involving the <a name="El2p3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Company other than the Merger, <a name="Elor3O"><!--Anchor--></a>(iii) corporate action the consummation of which would frustrate the purposes, or prevent or materially delay the consummation, of any <a name="Elqi3O"><!--Anchor--></a>of the transactions contemplated by the <a name="El2s3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Merger Agreement or <a name="Elou3O"><!--Anchor--></a>(iv) other matter relating to, or in connection with, any of the foregoing matters. Stockholder shall use its commercially reasonable efforts to ensure that, during the Support Period, any other Person having voting power with respect to any outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by Stockholder will not vote any such shares in favor of or consent to, and will vote against, the approval of the matters described in clauses (i) through (iv) of the preceding sentence.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Elov3O"><!--Anchor--></a></div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 2.02</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Irrevocable Proxy</font>.&#160; <a name="El2x3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder hereby revokes (or agrees to cause to be revoked) any and all previous proxies granted with respect to the outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <a name="El2b4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder.&#160; By entering into this <a name="El2y3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement, <a name="El2z3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder hereby grants a proxy appointing <a name="El2_3O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent as <a name="El2e4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder&#8217;s attorney-in-fact and proxy, with full power of substitution, for and in <a name="El204O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder&#8217;s name, to vote, express consent or dissent, or otherwise to utilize such voting power in the manner contemplated by Section 2.01<!--Anchor--> above as <a name="El214O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent or its proxy or substitute shall, in <a name="El224O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent&#8217;s sole discretion, deem proper with respect to the outstanding Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <a name="El2d4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder.&#160; The proxy granted by <a name="El234O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder pursuant to this Article 2<!--Anchor--> is irrevocable and is granted in consideration of <a name="El244O"><!--Anchor--></a>Parent and Acquisition Sub entering into this <a name="El254O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement and the <a name="El264O"><!--Anchor--></a>Merger Agreement and incurring certain related fees and expenses.&#160; The proxy granted by <a name="El274O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder shall not be exercised to vote, consent or act on any matter except as contemplated by Section 2.01<a name="Elli4O"><!--Anchor--></a> above.&#160; The proxy granted by <a name="El284O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder shall be revoked, terminated and of no further force or effect, automatically and without further action, upon termination of this <a name="El294O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement in accordance with Section 6.03 hereof.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt; FONT-WEIGHT: bold"><a name="Elol4O"><!--Anchor--></a>ARTICLE 3</div>

FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Authorization</font>.&#160; <a name="El9f5O"><!--Anchor--></a>The execution, delivery and performance by <a name="El2v4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder of this <a name="El2w4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement and the consummation by <a name="El2x4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder <a name="El9h5O"><!--Anchor--></a>of <a name="El9i5O"><!--Anchor--></a>the transactions contemplated hereby are within the powers of <a name="El2y4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder and, if applicable, <a name="El9k5O"><!--Anchor--></a>have been duly authorized by all necessary corporate, <a name="El2e5O"><!--Anchor--></a>company, partnership or other action.&#160; This <a name="El2z4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement constitutes a legal, valid and binding <a name="El2c5O"><!--Anchor--></a>agreement of <a name="El2_4O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder, enforceable against <a name="El205O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder <a name="El9m5O"><!--Anchor--></a>in accordance with its terms, subject to the effect of any applicable bankruptcy, insolvency, moratorium or similar law affecting creditors&#8217; rights generally, to rules of law governing specific performance, injunctive relief and other equitable remedies, to approval by the Company Board of this Agreement and the Merger Agreement and the transactions contemplated hereby and thereby for purposes of Section 203 of the DGCL and to the federal securities laws and rules promulgated thereunder, including but not limited to, any withdrawal rights under the tender offer rules.&#160; If this <a name="El285O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement is being executed in representative or fiduciary capacity, the Person signing this <a name="El2a5O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement has full power and authority to enter into and perform this <a name="El2b5O"><!--Anchor--></a>Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160;</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><a name="Elon6O"><!--Anchor--></a><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 3.03</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">&#160; Ownership of Shares</font>.&#160; <a name="El2p6O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder is the <a name="El2z6O"><!--Anchor--></a>Beneficial Owner of the Company <a name="El2_6O"><!--Anchor--></a><a name="El967O"><!--Anchor--></a>Shares <a name="El987O"><!--Anchor--></a>set forth on the signature page hereto opposite such <a name="El2u6O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder&#8217;s name, free and clear of any Lien and any other limitation or restriction (<a name="El237O"><!--Anchor--></a>including any restriction on the right to vote or otherwise dispose of the Company Shares Beneficially Owned by <a name="El217O"><!--Anchor--></a>Stockholder), except for any applicable restrictions on transfer under the federal or state securities laws and the rules and regulations promulgated thereunder that would not in any event prevent Stockholder from tendering Stockholder&#8217;s Company Shares in accordance with this Agreement or otherwise complying with Stockholder&#8217;s obligations under this Agreement.</div>

<div style="TEXT-ALIGN: justify; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt"><font style="FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">Section 3.06</font><font style="FONT-STYLE: italic; FONT-FAMILY: ''Times New Roman'', Times, serif; FONT-SIZE: 10pt">.&#160; No Litigation</font>.&#160; As of the date of this Agreement, there is no suit, claim, action, investigation or other Proceeding pending or, to the knowledge of Stockholder, threatened against Stockholder at law or in equity before or by any Governmental Authority that could reasonably be expected to impair the ability of Stockholder to perform Stockholder&#8217;s obligations hereunder or consummate the transactions contemplated hereby.</div>
